Overall layout:


Large, sprawling single-story villa with multiple interconnected sections
Mediterranean or Spanish-inspired architecture
Centered around an open courtyard with a pool


Exterior features:


Cream-colored stucco walls
Red terracotta tile roofs with multiple levels and angles
Large windows with wooden frames
Decorative wooden beams and supports
Stone or cobblestone foundation and accents


Courtyard:


Rectangular pool in the center, lined with quartz blocks
Wooden deck surrounding the pool
Various potted plants and flowers for decoration
Small fountain or water feature
Seating areas with chairs and tables


Main building sections:


Entrance area with a grand doorway and small porch
Living room with large windows facing the courtyard
Kitchen area with counters and appliances
Multiple bedrooms with private bathrooms
Study or library section


Outdoor areas:


Covered patio or pergola attached to the main building
Garden areas with various flowers, trees, and shrubs
Stone pathways connecting different sections of the property
Small vegetable or herb garden


Decorative elements:


Use of trapdoors and fences for window shutters and railings
Flower boxes under windows
Vines and leaves for added greenery on walls
Lanterns or other lighting fixtures for ambiance


Interior details:


Mixture of terracotta, wool, and wooden blocks for flooring
Comfortable seating areas with couches and chairs
Bookshelves and storage areas
Paintings and item frames for wall decorations
Proper lighting using a combination of torches, lanterns, and redstone lamps

Ensure the structure has a cohesive design that blends indoor and outdoor living spaces, with attention to detail in both the architecture and landscaping.
